<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Taboo桌游结合了复杂的词汇约束与沟通目标，适合作为分析LLM在同时应对规则遵守和交流效果时策略选择的研究场景。作者试图探索当前LLM在受限条件下的生成能力与人类表现之间的差距。

Method: 选用两个开源权重的大语言模型，从提示工程、生成时限制、内部表征操作三个层次，对模型输出进行干预。分别利用禁用词检测、LLM判断描述唤起目标词程度，并比较模型和人类在受限策略下的相似性。

Result: 不同干预条件下，模型在规则遵循与沟通效果之间表现出不同的权衡。但总体来看，模型对规则合规性和有效唤起目标词的表现远不如人类，作为猜测方弱势明显。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在受词汇约束条件下的词汇锚定（lexical grounding）和概念唤起仍是一大挑战，与人类表现有显著差距。对LLM在强约束交流环境中的能力提升仍有较大提升空间。

Abstract: The game of Taboo requires describing a target word without using a set of forbidden words, so that other players can guess it. This deceptively simple task combines strict lexical constraints with the need for communicatively effective descriptions, making it a compelling playground for examining how LLMs navigate competing demands at inference time. We evaluate two open-weight models under conditions that intervene at progressively deeper levels of the generative process, from prompting to generation-time constraints to internal representations manipulations. We assess their outputs through forbidden word violation detection, LLM-as-a-judge measuring the degree to which generated descriptions successfully evoke the target concept for both human and machine guessers, and examining whether the strategies models adopt under constraint align with those of human players. Our results show that compliance with the rules of the game and communicative effectiveness trade off differently across conditions, and that models remain substantially weaker than humans as guessers, suggesting that lexical grounding under constraint is an open challenge for current language models.

### [169] [Auditing Forgetting in Limited Memory Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00605)
*Arya Raeesi,Hanna Roed*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种因果审计框架，用于评估有限记忆语言模型（LMLMs）在外部知识库事实删除后的表现，并揭示残留事实主要来源于检索路径而非模型参数记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前用于评估LMLMs事实删除效果的方法无法精确区分知识消除效果，例如无法判断删除的事实是否仍然以模型参数记忆、检索路径偏差或邻近检索伪影的形式残留。为推动可控知识删除，提高模型安全性与可解释性，需要更细致的审计工具与分析方法。

Method: 作者提出了一套因果审计框架，通过在推理阶段保持模型参数不变，仅变更数据库状态（FULL、DEL-ON、DEL-OFF三种干预），来细粒度地分解知识删除后的三种行为：参数泄漏、检索介导正确性、检索伪影率。该方法在13类数据库、4种对抗拓扑（Base、Alias、Noise、Collision）和6种提示方式下，对12,228项别名闭包删除进行全面实验分析。

Result: 实验发现：无论数据库拓扑还是提示方式如何，参数泄漏（模型记忆中遗漏事实）几乎为零；而事实删除后残存的正确回答主要来自于检索路径（检索介导的正确性和检索伪影率几乎重合），即邻近检索导致答案复现，其比例在不同数据库从0.7%到13.6%不等。

Conclusion: 对于当前LMLM及对应的事实删除流程来说，知识被遗忘的界限主要由数据库管理而非模型自身决定。提示工程无法进一步单独影响已删除事实的残留。改进知识消除效果，需在数据库结构和检索层面发力。

Abstract: Limited Memory Language Models (LMLMs) externalize factual knowledge to a database to enable deletion-based unlearning without retraining. Existing evaluations measure post-deletion correctness in aggregate and cannot tell whether a deleted fact persists through residual parametric memory, alternative retrieval paths, or near-neighbor retrieval artifacts. We propose a causal auditing framework that holds the model fixed and varies the database state at inference time across three interventions: FULL, DEL-ON, and DEL-OFF. The framework decomposes post-deletion behavior into parametric leakage L(f), retrieval-mediated correctness R(f), and a retrieval artifact rate grounded in the inference-time retrieval trace. We apply it to 12,228 alias-closure deletions across thirteen databases, including four adversarial topologies (Base, Alias, Noise, Collision) we construct in three domains, and six prompt formulations. Parametric leakage is near zero in every variant and every prompt style: the model rarely returns the deleted answer in the absence of retrieval. The residual that does survive lives in the retrieval graph: retrieval-mediated correctness and the retrieval artifact rate match within rounding everywhere, so post-deletion correctness is, in our audit, predominantly reconstituted from near-neighbor retrieval. This residual ranges from 0.7% on the released LMLM database to 13.6% on the most adversarial variant, and prompt formulation does not independently control how much of a deleted fact survives. These results suggest that, for this class of LMLM and deletion procedure, the unlearning boundary is drawn primarily by the database administrator rather than by the model.

</details>

*Frank Xing,Erik Cambria*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对事件驱动情感分析的解释接口，利用显式的规则和可验证的推理流程提升模型结果的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的情感分类模型大多在输出标签后才进行解释，难以确保解释反映了真实计算过程，难以进行因果验证和人工审查。为解决这一缺陷，作者希望通过建立更透明、因果可验证的方法提升情感分类的可解释性和可审计性。

Method: 作者设计了一个基于事件的情感分析接口，核心方法包括：1）构建解析器将文本映射为使用自然语义元语言（NSM）的短剧本，共12个类型化槽位；2）使用完全公开的规则列表根据该剧本直接计算情感标签，实现由定义驱动的可解释推理；3）所有与经验风险相关的问题集中在学习型解析器，明确分离推理与感知环节。

Result: 在众包收集的事件描述数据上，微调后的解析器在一个小型持出集上取得了0.33的准确率和0.48的选择性准确率。实验结果表明，该方案在可验证性、可解释性提升的同时，准确率与黑盒模型差异不大。

Conclusion: 本文提出的解释接口能够以因果和定义为依据提供可审查的决策过程，实现事件驱动情感分析的透明化。公开了EmoExpl-1200数据集及全部决策规则，为未来相关研究提供了基础。

Abstract: Explanations for emotion classifiers are usually produced post hoc, with no guarantee that they reflect the computation behind the label. We present an explication interface for event-based emotion analysis. A parser maps the input text to an explication, a short script in the closed vocabulary of Natural Semantic Metalanguage organized into twelve typed slots, and a fixed decision list of rules transcribed from published semantic definitions computes the label from the explication alone. The faithfulness guarantee is therefore causal and definitional, while all empirical risk lives in the learned parser, which the per-line entailment interface makes auditable against the input. On crowd-sourced event descriptions, our fine-tuned parser reaches 0.33 accuracy and 0.48 selective accuracy on a small held-out set, suggesting that the interface trades insignificant accuracy difference to a black-box model for a verifiable, inspectable decision basis for first-person event-based emotion analysis. We also release EmoExpl-1200 with per-line verification metadata and the full rule set.

### [172] [Self-conditioned Flow Map Language Models via Fixed-point Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00714)
*Jaehoon Yoo,Wonjung Kim,Floor Eijkelboom,Chanhyuk Lee,Nicholas M. Boffi,Seunghoon Hong,Jinwoo Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的自条件化流语言模型（FMLM*），通过引入定点迭代理论，提升了语言模型的效率和生成质量，并在OpenWebText数据集上的一步或少步生成任务中优于当前最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自条件化在提升流模型表现上展现出实证优势，但其提升机制并不透明，且当前对于如何将其用于少步生成还不明确。本文希望深入理解自条件化的工作原理，并设计能够高效应用于少步生成的新模型框架。

Method: 作者提出以定点迭代视角分析自条件化流模型，进而提出了‘定点流’（fixed-point flows）的新类别：它在两个维度上（流过程与定点迭代）组织信息。并设计模型蒸馏方法，分别针对定点迭代和流过程进行模型压缩，最终得到高效的FMLM*模型。

Abstract: Self-conditioning is a core technique that enhances continuous flow-based language models, where the model learns to denoise generated text by conditioning on its own denoising estimate. While empirically successful, its performance improvements are poorly understood. Moreover, there is growing interest in the use of few-step generators based on flow maps, for which how to leverage self-conditioning is unclear. Here, we show that flow language models with self-conditioning solve a fixed-point iteration that bootstraps the performance of the learned denoiser. We use this viewpoint to formulate fixed-point flows, a two-dimensional class of self-conditioned flows, where the first dimension represents the flow process and the second represents the fixed-point iteration. We show that fixed-point flows define valid flow maps, and show that they can be distilled from self-conditioned flow models by compressing both fixed-point iterations and the flow process, the former with fixed-point distillation and the latter with flow map distillation. Our resulting flow map language model, FMLM$^\star$, outperforms state-of-the-art self-conditioned models and few-step models in one- and few-step generation on OpenWebText. Code is available at https://github.com/Ugness/self-conditioned-fmlm.

### [173] [MSQA: A Natively Sourced Multilingual and Multicultural SimpleQA Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00724)
*Xianru Chen,Yukai Huang,Mingxiang Chen,Xinping Lei,Fangbing Deng,Jin Chen,Ge Zhang,Wenhao Huang,Jiaheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多语言大模型（LLMs）能够以用户母语交流并不意味着它们具备该语言背后的文化理解，并提出MSQA基准测试集来系统性地检验这一点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前普遍认为，能流利使用多种语言的语言模型也能理解相关文化，但这一假设从未被系统性验证。作者希望通过实证研究测试这种“文化一致性”的假象。

Method: 作者构建了MSQA基准，包括11种语言、5种文化维度、3个难度层级，共1064个本地撰写问题，针对本地知识，减少英译带来的偏差。以该数据集测试了18种大语言模型，并分析多种推理优化策略如校准、采样、检索增强的效果。

Result: 实验发现，大模型的文化理解能力随着预训练时的本地语言暴露量变化大，不依赖一般推理能力，并存在明显的“局域性效应”；推理时的常用补救手段对提升文化对齐效果有限，模型在陌生文化问题上表现过度自信，重复采样结果不稳定，检索增强对部分长尾事实表现不均。

Conclusion: 多语言能力并不代表拥有相应文化理解，当前推理时常用手段难以解决这一错觉，要实现真正的文化对齐仍需更深层的技术干预。

Abstract: Multilingual fluency often invites a stronger assumption: a model that can speak a user's language must also understand the culture encoded by that language. We call this the Illusion of Cultural Alignment. To test this assumption directly, we introduce MSQA, a benchmark of 1,064 natively sourced questions across 11 language groups, five cultural dimensions, and three difficulty tiers. Unlike translated benchmarks, MSQA targets locally grounded knowledge and reduces shortcuts from English-centric cross-lingual transfer. Evaluating 18 LLMs, we find substantial cultural degradation and a pronounced Locality Effect: cultural competence tracks pre-training exposure more closely than general reasoning ability. We further show that common inference-time remedies do not dissolve the illusion. Models remain overconfident on unfamiliar cultural questions, repeated sampling yields unstable rather than reliable correctness, and retrieval augmentation helps unevenly on long-tail facts. These findings indicate that cultural alignment cannot be inferred from multilingual ability alone and requires deeper intervention than calibration, sampling, or retrieval at inference time

</details>


### [174] [What Survives Into Context: A Diagnostic for Budget-Constrained Multi-Hop RAG and When Submodular Evidence Packing Improves It](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00725)
*Ananto Nayan Bala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文讨论了RAG任务下，固定阅读上下文长度导致仅能选择部分检索文档，提出“answer-in-context”（答案在上下文中出现）比传统的文档召回率指标更能预测最终问答效果，并设计了优化上下文打包的算法，在特定条件下显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型RAG系统通常用检索文档召回率作为评价指标，但实际只允许有限文档输入阅读器，召回率与最终准确性关联度低，需要更相关的衡量方法和优化算法。

Method: 1）提出“answer-in-context”指标，衡量正确答案是否以连续片段出现在输入给阅读器的上下文中。2）将上下文构建建模为预算受限的单调子模最大化问题，联合优化相关性、覆盖率、多样性等，设计高效pack算法选择输入片段。3）多数据集实验和受控变量分析。

Result: “answer-in-context”能更好地预测答案F1，与召回相比解释力提高，且能区分答案质量。在HotpotQA数据集上，所提Pack算法在160-token输入预算下，F1值提升最高达5.1分，且消耗token更少。在特定条件（如多跳结构、证据可被检索、预算中等、阅读器能力有限）下表现最优。

Conclusion: 优化reader context的答案覆盖比单纯提升召回更有效；算法提升受条件约束，阅读器模型强大后收益消失；提出的answer-in-context指标对理解和优化RAG系统有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) under a fixed reader-context budget forces a selection problem: of the evidence retrieved, only a fraction can be shown to the reader. We argue that document recall -- the standard retrieval metric -- is the wrong quantity to optimize in this regime, and we make two contributions. First, as a general contribution, we introduce answer-in-context, a diagnostic that measures whether a gold answer survives as a contiguous span in the packed reader context (not the retrieved set). It predicts answer F1 better than recall (r=0.39-0.55 vs. about 0.31), separates answer quality roughly five-fold (0.60 vs. 0.12 on HotpotQA), and carries information beyond retrieval: it adds Delta R squared=0.17 over recall and shows a 4.6x EM gap even among questions where all gold was retrieved. We also confirm it interventionally: on 2WikiMultiHopQA a packing change that raises coverage but not answer-in-context yields no accuracy gain. Second, as a conditional contribution, we cast reader-context construction as budgeted monotone submodular maximization and build a packer that jointly optimizes relevance, query coverage, representativeness, and diversity. On HotpotQA with a 160-token budget and a 3B reader it beats a strong focused heuristic, MMR, and naive packing -- by up to +5.1 F1 at equal-or-lower token cost, across three seeds. Crucially, we map the scope of this win honestly: it requires the conjunction of (i) multi-hop complementary structure, (ii) retrieval that surfaces the evidence, (iii) a binding but not extreme budget, and (iv) a reader weak enough that evidence density, not reading capacity, is the bottleneck. A quantization-controlled reader-scale ladder (3B to 7B to 14B) shows the edge over the heuristic is absorbed by 7B and significantly reverses by 14B, while the diagnostic explains every boundary with a single variable.

</details>

The original corpora we used are monolingual, where we carried out error annotation using the MetaHOPE framework, and also produced the human post-edited gold reference for bilingual use as a new resource. We believe the MetaHOPE evaluation framework for metaphor translation annotation, the parallel corpora resources, and the error analysis on SOTA automatic translation models can be useful and shed some light for the field of metaphor translation study. ### [177] [Recovering Input Text from Hidden States: Study of Gradient-Based Inversion of Decoder-Only Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00852)
*Mikołaj Słowikowski,Maciej Witold Majewski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了从解码器语言模型最后一层隐藏状态中恢复原始输入序列的问题，并用连续嵌入空间优化的方法进行分析，揭示了重建准确率的提升及影响因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型广泛应用于文本生成及各种自然语言处理任务，人们日益关注其隐藏状态泄露的风险。本研究旨在系统分析隐藏状态到原始文本的可逆性，并评估不同方法在恢复原始输入时的表现与特点。

Method: 作者不采用一刀切的直接还原方法，而是使用连续嵌入空间中的优化过程：优化在嵌入空间中持续进行，只在内部搜索循环的最后一步才离散化成具体token。同时，文章跟踪ground-truth token的rank变化、计算每步损失曲线，并统计commit时的离散误差，以此揭示隐藏状态重建的详细过程。

Result: 实验显示，对于10-token的C4数据集输入，通过扩大候选窗口，精确匹配率从66.9%提升到97.5%（平均相似度0.994）。分析发现，出错主要集中在以空格开头且高频的功能性词（如介词、连词等），而具有关键信息的内容词几乎可完美恢复。与现有SIPIT方法对比，连续方法虽慢但更易于分析优化过程和识别失败原因。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了GPT-2最后一层隐藏状态对原始文本高度敏感，大多数恢复失败并非真正歧义而是“接近匹配”；连续优化方法适合分析模型重建能力及其存在的局限。

Abstract: This work studies the hidden-state inversion problem: recovering the original input token sequence of a decoder-only language model from its last-layer hidden states. Rather than treating inversion as a one-shot reconstruction, we study it as a continuous embedding-space optimisation in which a soft proxy is driven towards the leaked target without any hard-token projection during the search, and a token is committed only once, at the end of the inner loop. This design choice has two consequences which are the main focus of this paper. First, keeping the optimisation entirely in continuous space exposes a rich set of internal signals: rank trajectories of the ground-truth token, per-position loss curves, and a discrete loss measured at commit time. Second, the discrete loss allows assessing the correctness of recovery via cumulative discrete loss. We further analyse which tokens break the reconstructions and find a sharp categorical asymmetry: space-prefixed, high-frequency function words in dense regions of the embedding matrix dominate the failures, while content-bearing tokens are recovered almost perfectly. On 10-token C4 prompts the exact-match rate rises from 66.9% to 97.5% (mean similarity 0.994) as the candidate window is widened, confirming that most errors are recoverable near-misses rather than genuine ambiguities. A comparison with the released SIPIT reference situates these findings: per-step hard projection is faster, but the continuous formulation is what makes the optimisation observable and its failures detectable. The results show that last-layer hidden states of GPT-2 are as sensitive as the original text.

</details>


### [178] [CAT: Confidence-Adaptive Thinking for Efficient Reasoning of Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00862)
*Qizhi Jiang,Shuo Wang,Pei Ke,Yuhang Song,Ke Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自适应推理长度的新方法CAT，可根据问题难度动态调整大规模推理模型（LRMs）推理时的回答长度，从而提升简单问题上的效率，同时在复杂问题上维持高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LRMs在处理简单问题时通常会“过度思考”，造成推理冗余和推断效率下降。现有压缩方法不能有效区分问题难度，有可能损失复杂问题上的性能。

Method: 提出Confidence-Adaptive Thinking（CAT）框架，通过引入模型对自身预测置信度的自适应信号，在推理过程中动态调节推理链长度。CAT将置信度纳入偏好优化，使模型对高置信度（简单问题）产生更简短的推理，对低置信度（复杂问题）产生更充分的推理。

Result: 在多个基准数据集和不同基座模型上，CAT显著提升了推理准确率，其性能优于当前最先进的基线方法。实验表明，CAT能有效在保持准确性的同时压缩冗余推理，加快推断速度。

Conclusion: CAT方法为LRMs提供了兼顾推理准确性与延迟的新思路，能在实际工业场景中高效处理不同难度的问题，具有较强的实用价值。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have achieved remarkable success on complex tasks by leveraging long chain-of-thought (CoT) trajectories, yet they frequently exhibit overthinking on simple queries, resulting in significant token overhead and reduced inference efficiency. However, existing compression methods predominantly apply uniform length reduction or rely on coarse-grained difficulty estimation, often leading to performance degradation on difficult problems. To address this limitation, we propose Confidence-Adaptive Thinking (CAT), a framework that incorporates the model's intrinsic self-certainty signals as confidence into the preference optimization process, which autonomously modulates reasoning lengths based on problem difficulty. Experimental results show that CAT consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on reasoning accuracy across multiple benchmarks on different base models. Our work enables LRMs to effectively compress confident responses while deliberating on uncertain ones, offering a potentially robust solution for balancing accuracy and latency in practical industrial scenarios.

### [179] [Dynamic Bidirectional Pattern Memory: A Production-Scale Empirical Characterisation of Inference-Time Gating in Clinical NLP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00870)
*Ali H. Lazem,William Teahan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了临床NLP流水线中推理阶段模式记忆门控，评估了不同过滤机制对生成-校验结构的改进效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模临床文本抽取任务中，生成-校验流水线常需反复校验已被拒绝过的信息，影响效率，因此尝试通过记忆机制减少重复劳动。

Method: 流水线由Llama-3.3 70B生成器与MMed-Llama-3.1 70B校验器组成，并在部署时加入轻量级“记忆”，用于学习过滤机制。实验比较了学习型过滤、基于临床本体的规则、以及五种问答式过滤方案在海量数据上的表现。

Result: （1）直接学习校验器的拒绝例无法累计有效过滤规则；（2）基于本体规则能同样过滤无效关系；（3）五种问答式过滤中仅“是否支持提问”方案有效，能明显提升过滤准确性；（4）只有考察实际证据的过滤器才具备选择性，单纯模仿校验器输出是无效的。

Conclusion: 对任何生成-校验型流水线，最直观的记忆机制在大规模下可能完全失效，能否有效过滤由机制是否专注于与校验器关注点一致的证据决定。全流程保持可审查性，数据开放。

Abstract: We study inference-time pattern-memory gating in a production-scale clinical natural language processing (NLP) pipeline. The pipeline pairs a generator (Llama-3.3 70B) proposing extractions with a verifier (MMed-Llama-3.1 70B) accepting or rejecting them, over 167,034 PMC-Patients narratives, and adds a lightweight memory that learns at deployment which extractions to filter, so the verifier need not re-examine candidates already seen to fail. We report four findings. First, learning filtering rules directly from the verifier's rejections failed at full scale: the relation-extraction filter stayed empty despite 785,797 logged rejections, because they were spread too thinly across too many distinct forms to accumulate. Second, a simpler rule using a fixed clinical ontology produced the same filtering without the verifier, capturing 49,734 ontology-violating relations on a held-out 5,000-patient set. Third, of five versions of the question-answering filter, four failed for distinct, instructive reasons; the fifth succeeded by checking whether a patient's extracted entities support the question asked, and where it applies was 1.84 times likelier to flag an answer the verifier would reject than one it would accept. Fourth, one pattern held across all five: a filter is selective only when it tests the same evidence the verifier weighs, not when it imitates the verifier's output. Together these give a transferable result for any generator-verifier pipeline: the most natural memory design can fail silently at scale, and whether a pre-generation gate is selective is decided before any engineering effort, by whether its signal probes the question the verifier itself answers. Throughout, the system flags suspect extractions rather than deleting them, so every decision stays visible for clinical review. All code and test artefacts are released openly.

Abstract: Rhetorical strategies and their influence on audiences are often studied through social media posts and comments. This study investigates how two classical modes of persuasion, ethos and pathos, resonate in the silent audience's interpretations of meaning. Using a dataset of social media sentences paired with human-written interpretations, we label both sources for ethos and pathos and assess whether these rhetorical appeals are preserved. Our analyses show that interpretations diverge from the original sentences in 30% of cases, with rhetorically charged content eliciting greater variability than neutral content. We further find that ethos and pathos in original sentences can predict audience attitudes toward the author, underscoring the subtle ways rhetoric shapes perception beyond visible engagement.

Abstract: Open web-scale pre-training corpora remain concentrated in English, limiting multilingual LLM development. We introduce MultiSynt/MT, an open synthetic parallel corpus with approximately 4.8 trillion target-language tokens across 36 European languages, produced by translating 100 billion high-quality Nemotron-CC tokens with Tower+ and OPUS-MT/HPLT-MT systems. For many medium- and lower-resource European languages, this is the largest openly available pre-training resource. On a broad multilingual benchmark suite, reference LLMs trained on MultiSynt/MT reach the final score of HPLT 2.0, a native-data baseline, using roughly 72% fewer pre-training tokens, and outperform it by approximately 15% relative at a matched 100B-token training budget. Our analyses also identify evaluation blind spots: standard multiple-choice benchmarks miss translation-quality differences that a fluency-sensitive LLM-as-judge evaluation cleanly recovers on the trained LLMs (with no fluency deficit in MultiSynt itself), and Norwegian idiomatic and culturally grounded tasks remain better served by native data. We release the corpus, including row-aligned translations from multiple systems, to support controlled research on multilingual pre-training data and evaluation.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的基准，用于评估面向结构化输入（如代码、工具输出、表格等）和自然语言文档的RAG（检索增强生成）系统中的幻觉检测能力，并验证其有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前RAG幻觉检测研究大多集中在自然语言文档上，而实际系统越来越多地涉及结构化输入如代码、开发者工具输出及元数据，缺少针对多样输入类型的评公开准确评测方法。

Method: 作者构建了涵盖代码、工具输出、结构化文档与自然语言的统一基准。具体方法为：以有确凿证据的正确答案为基础，注入精准定位的局部幻觉，并对代码部分进行证据评审。同时，微调Qwen3.5-2B模型用于检测幻觉，并与现有方法如LettuceDetect-large和零样本LLM裁判进行对比。

Result: 微调后的Qwen3.5-2B模型在统一测试集上获得0.689的span-F1值，在代码代理数据上达到0.60，显著优于LettuceDetect-large（0.17）和零样本LLM裁判（最高0.22）。在自然语言已有基准上也表现不俗（RAGTruth example-F1为81.8、PsiloQA IoU为0.724）。

Conclusion: 文中统一基准与模型方法提升了复杂多源输入场景下的幻觉检测能力，为后续相关研究及实际系统评测提供了有力工具和参考。

Abstract: Hallucination detection for retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is usually evaluated on natural-language document evidence. However, grounded generation systems increasingly rely on structured inputs: source code, developer-tool output, markdown documents, tables, and repository metadata. We introduce a unified benchmark for span-level hallucination detection over code, tool output, structured documents, and existing natural-language RAG datasets. The benchmark is built by starting from grounded correct answers, injecting localized hallucinations with exact character labels, and validating the code test split with evidence-based review. Our fine-tuned Qwen3.5-2B detector reaches 0.689 span-F1 on the unified test set and 0.60 on the code-agent source, where it substantially outperforms LettuceDetect-large (0.17) and the strongest zero-shot LLM judges we evaluated (at most 0.22). The same model remains competitive on established natural-language benchmarks, with 81.8 RAGTruth example-F1 and 0.724 English PsiloQA IoU.

### [183] [From Personas to Plot: Character-Grounded Multi-Agent Story Generation for Long-Form Narratives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00918)
*Aayush Aluru,Chloe Ho,Muhammad Hammouri,Kerry Luo,Myra Malik,Ryan Lagasse,Arjun Bahuguna,Vasu Sharma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了MAGNET和ATLAS两个方法，旨在解决大型语言模型（LLM）在长篇故事生成中情节连贯和一致性差的问题。实验显示该框架能显著减少幻觉和注释错误，提升叙事连贯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在创作虚构故事方面表现出色，但在长篇故事中难以保持角色和情节的一致性和连贯。为解决此问题，作者提出需要更结构化和可控的生成框架。

Method: 提出MAGNET（多智能体基于目标的叙事引擎），通过具有人设的角色智能体在共享世界和动态故事目标下生成动作；同时引入ATLAS（基于图的管线），用于对比不同场景的世界状态以检测幻觉。

Result: 与单模型和IBSEN方法相比，MAGNET在100页规模下注释减少41%、幻觉减少50%，相较于IBSEN减少34%和45%。基于评测量表的双向评价也证实了本框架的优越性。

Conclusion: 显示通过显式的世界状态追踪和基于目标的多智能体生成，可以有效产生结构连贯、可控的长篇叙事，为长篇连贯生成奠定了方法基础。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive creative fiction generation, they struggle to maintain narrative consistency and coherent plot lines in long-form stories. In this work, we introduce a unified framework for long-form narrative generation and verification. MAGNET, a multi-agent goal-driven narrative engine for storytelling, generates stories with persona-grounded character agents that propose actions based on a shared world state and evolving story goals, while ATLAS is a graph-based pipeline that compares scene-level world representations across a generated story to detect hallucinations. By evaluating MAGNET using an LLM editor, pairwise rubric scoring, and ATLAS, we show that our framework produces coherent narratives compared to single-model prompting and IBSEN. At 100 pages, MAGNET reduced annotations and hallucinations by 41 and 50%, respectively, compared to the single model baseline and by 34 and 45%, respectively, compared to IBSEN, with pairwise rubric evaluation showing similar results. These results suggest that long-form narratives can emerge from explicit world-state tracking and goal-driven multi-agent generation, providing a foundation for controllable and structurally coherent long-form narrative generation.

### [184] [Persona Non Grata: LLM Persona-Driven Generations in MCQA are Unstable in Distinct Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00937)
*César Guerra-Solano,Xiang Lorraine Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文研究了大语言模型（LLM）在扮演特定人物（persona）进行选择题任务（MCQA）时的不稳定性，并提出了用于量化该不稳定性的三类指标。实验发现，不同模型、领域和任务设置对输出稳定性有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往关于persona驱动生成的研究多关注对话等文本任务中角色一致性，但对于选择题等非文本型输出中的表现和稳定性探究较少。论文希望填补这一领域空白，了解并量化大语言模型在MCQA场景下的persona不稳定性。

Method: 作者设计并提出了三种度量MCQA任务中persona驱动生成稳定性的指标，分别从模型表现、结果一致性和问题正确性三方面进行评估。通过改变模型类型、模型规模、题目领域和任务设定等多种变量，系统性评测其对稳定性的影响。

Result: 实验表明：1）不同模型系列、规模对稳定性差异较大；2）题目领域如数学和常识类带来更高的不稳定性；3）任务的prompt格式引入的输出不稳定性比温度等超参更高；4）模型准确率和稳定性相关，根据稳定性指标，最佳/最差persona的选取还依赖设置不同。

Conclusion: 作者强调在persona驱动生成任务中，应该充分关注和排查超参数等设置导致的输出不稳定问题，以获得可重复、可信赖的模型表现。

Abstract: Persona-driven generations (PDGs) have seen prolific use in research and industry applications, where a large language model (LLM) takes on a 'persona' while completing some task. While persona expressed through free-form text (like dialogue) has substantial work investigating stability or consistency, relatively, persona expressed in non-text-heavy outputs (like in multiple-choice question answering, or MCQA) is often overlooked. We work to address this gap, seeking to understand the instability of LLM PDGs in MCQA tasks. We develop three metrics investigating the performance, outcome, and question correctness stability, evaluating three distinct dimensions. Using these metrics, we find that instability varies consistently between model families and model size, and across question domains, with math/commonsense questions leading to greater instability. We also find task prompt format introduces more prediction instability than other hyperparameters, like temperature. Finally, we find that instability is related to task accuracy, and using our instability metrics, find different experimental settings that result in different best and worst personas for tasks, despite their similarity. This reveals the importance of checking hyperparameter instability in PDGs.

Method: 利用131,306条句子、13类情感的boltuix/emotions数据集，随机抽取1000句组成测试集，对Claude、ChatGPT和Gemini三个主流大模型进行零样本同一提示的情感分类评测，并进行了统计学显著性检验。

Abstract: Emotion recognition in natural language is a foundational challenge in affective computing, with critical implications for human-computer interaction, mental health support, and conversational AI. The models were queried through their respective production APIs as of April 2026 on a fine-grained 13-class emotion classification task. Using a stratified 1,000-sentence sample from the boltuix/emotions dataset, which comprises 131,306 sentences across 13 categories, a single uniform prompt with no exemplars was applied identically across all models. Gemini achieves the highest accuracy (39.9%) and macro-F1 score (0.363), followed by GPT-5.4 (38.8%, macro-F1 = 0.291) and Claude (38.0%, macro-F1 = 0.159). All models excel on sarcasm and desire while consistently failing on love, confusion, and shame. McNemar tests reveal no statistically significant pairwise differences (p > 0.10), suggesting convergence at a shared zero-shot ceiling. Claude's markedly lower macro-F1 score exposes a class-imbalance prediction bias. These findings highlight the current limitations of frontier AI systems in zero-shot fine-grained emotion classification.

This platform is built upon SQLite FTS5 full-text indexes provided via a FastAPI backend, deployed as Docker containers on Azure, and released under the MIT license. Source code, build scripts, and deployment configurations are publicly available on GitHub. Users can add their own corpora and deploy their own instances. This document describes the system design, corpus structure, and use cases demonstrating the various queries supported by the platform. Svarna serves as the first step in exploring available data and is expected to lay the foundation for more comprehensive research in the future.

### [188] [Logit-Contribution Scoring Identifies Non-Literal Retrieval Heads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01002)
*Aryo Pradipta Gema,Beatrice Alex,Pasquale Minervini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了LOCOS方法，可检测大模型中进行非字面检索/综合信息的关注头，并显著优于以往基于匹配的检测器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型处理长上下文时，并非简单复制答案，而是综合理解、检索相关信息。识别哪些attention head具备此能力对模型可解释性和行为理解很重要。但现有检测器基于是否“抄写”答案而定义，这忽略了attention head通过输出值（OV-circuit）实现的信息综合功能。

Method: 提出Logit-Contribution Scoring（LOCOS），它关注于attention head输出值在答案token嵌入方向上的投影分数，并通过对比“针”（答案相关）与“非针”（答案无关）位置，实现对关键head的单次前向检测。

Result: 在Qwen3、Gemma-3、OLMo-3.1三大模型家族上，相比旧方法，LOCOS检测到的top head更具决定性：在NoLiMa基准上，只需消融LOCOS筛选的50个head，ROUGE-L分数则从0.401降到0，而强基线方法仍有0.292。消融这些head对模型“检索”能力影响巨大，但不会影响参数记忆或算术推理。同样消融在MuSiQue和BABI-Long任务上ROUGE-L也大幅下降，随机消融无此现象。

Conclusion: LOCOS可精准发现负责信息检索/综合的attention head，这为长文本大模型的可解释性分析和模型行为干预提供了新工具，显著改进了对非字面检索机制的检测能力。

Abstract: In long-context use, large language models frequently synthesize answers from the meaning of a relevant context span rather than literally copy-pasting them. Identifying which attention heads perform this synthesis matters for interpreting long-context model behavior. Yet existing detectors miss these heads by construction: they reward heads whose attended token matches the generated token, a literal-copy criterion that captures where a head reads but not what it writes through its output-value (OV) circuit, the very mechanism that carries non-literal retrieval. We introduce Logit-Contribution Scoring (LOCOS), a write-aware detector that scores each head by the projection of its OV-circuit output onto the answer-token unembedding direction, contrasting needle and off-needle source positions in a single forward pass. Across three model families (Qwen3, Gemma-3, OLMo-3.1), mean-ablating the top LOCOS heads on the NoLiMa non-literal retrieval benchmark collapses ROUGE-L at lower head counts than prior attention-based detections; on Qwen3-8B, ablating 50 heads drives ROUGE-L from 0.401 to 0.000 while the strongest baseline still retains 0.292. The selected heads are retrieval-specific: parametric recall and arithmetic reasoning stay at baseline under the same ablation. On Qwen3-8B, the same ablation also drops MuSiQue from 0.55 to 0.08 and BABI-Long from 0.62 to 0.20, while a random-heads control stays within 0.05 of baseline.

</details>


### [189] [Understanding Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01006)
*Yannik Keller,Thomas Eisenmann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文综述了大语言模型（LLMs）的主要进展、机制、与人类认知的关系及当前关于其认知能力的争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在AI和自然语言处理领域取得了重大突破，但其内部机制、能力边界和与人类认知的关系存在大量未解之谜和争议。该章节旨在梳理现有证据，澄清这些核心问题。

Method: 文章首先总体回顾了Transformer结构，尤其是注意力机制如何推动模型泛化能力。接着，分析了LLMs展现出类似人类认知的能力（如符号推理、心理理论、欺骗策略等），并讨论了部分LLMs在原认为人类独有的认知任务上的表现及其失败案例。文章还梳理了用于解释AI的主要方法，如神经元激活分析和回路追踪。最后，分析了有关LLMs“理解力”与“表面模仿”的争议，并对现有反人类化观点进行批评。

Result: LLMs在部分任务上展现出接近或类似人类认知的表现，甚至能完成以往被认为仅依赖人类智能的任务。同时，研究也揭示了模型与人类在认知本质上的显著不同和典型失误。解释性研究推动了模型机制的理解，但仍有许多存疑之处。

Conclusion: 作者主张应以更细致和辩证的视角审视LLMs的“智力”与理解，既要看到其与人类认知的区别，也不应以极端简化的论点彻底否定AI认知的可能性，推动对LLMs认知本质的深入探讨。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) represent one of the most significant advances in AI and natural language processing in recent years. Still, many pressing questions about their mechanisms, capabilities, and relationship to human cognition remain highly debated. This chapter aims to outline our current understanding of LLMs by discussing recent evidence on emerging capabilities and their mechanistic implementation within processing layers. We begin with a concise overview of the Transformer architecture, emphasizing how the attention mechanism enables training on massive datasets, allowing LLMs to function as generalist rather than specialized models. Next, we examine emergent LLM capabilities that appear to resemble aspects of human cognition, including symbolic reasoning, theory of mind, and deception strategies. Several studies provide evidence that LLMs can solve tasks previously thought to require human-like cognition. Other studies reveal insightful failure cases that shed light on the differences between human and LLM cognition. Alongside these findings, we review explainable AI approaches ranging from neuron activation analysis to circuit tracing. In the final section, we address current debates concerning what LLMs genuinely understand versus what they merely appear to understand. Prominent arguments against AI anthropomorphism point to the simplicity of LLM training objectives, claiming that LLM behavior is better explained by pattern memorization of training data than by genuine cognition. We argue that this standpoint is guided by misconceptions about optimization processes and cognitive capacity, and advocate for a more nuanced discussion of LLM cognition that neither dismisses the differences between humans and LLMs nor precludes the possibility of AI cognition through overly simplistic reductionist arguments.

</details>


### [190] [Reading Order Inference for Complex Document Layouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01018)
*Iddo Hakim,Sharva Gogawale,Omer Ventura,Gal Grudka,Daria Vasyutinsky-Shapira,Berat Kurar-Barakat,Nachum Dershowitz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需训练的基于图的阅读顺序推断方法，显著提升了复杂历史手稿多流排版下的阅读顺序识别准确率，特别是在Glossa Ordinaria等环绕式布局场景中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂历史手稿的数字化中，含有多个空间交错阅读流的页面（如Glossa Ordinaria的中心正文和包围注释）使得准确推断阅读顺序变得极具挑战性，现有方法在非规则、非矩形区域的处理上表现不佳。

Method: 将OCR文本行作为有向图的节点，通过加权组合两种轻量级语言模型信号（生成式语言模型的条件概率和BERT的NSP），为节点间候选转移（边）打分，最终通过度限制有向路径覆盖恢复全局阅读顺序，并提出max-regret推断来避免贪心算法中的错误累积。

Result: 在合成Glossa布局、23个ALTO页面几何及OmniDocBench多栏子集上，与XY-cut和两种LayoutReader方法对比，提出方法在Glossa布局能恢复95%的真实后继边，OmniDocBench子集准确率达88%，明显优于现有方法；其镜像不变性能也表现更好。

Conclusion: 新方法在复杂多流文本布局下具备显著的准确率和稳健性优势，为历史文献数字化中的阅读顺序推断提供了更可靠的工具，优于主流基线模型。

Abstract: Reading order inference remains a critical bottleneck in the digitization of complex historical manuscripts, where pages contain multiple spatially interleaved reading streams, the canonical example being the Glossa Ordinaria layout, in which a central text is surrounded by commentaries that wrap around it in non-rectangular, non-convex regions. We present a training-free, graph-based framework: each OCR text line becomes a node in a directed candidate-transition graph, edges are scored by a weighted additive ensemble of two lightweight language-model signals (causal language model conditional likelihood and BERT next-sentence prediction, NSP; a third sentence-embedding signal was evaluated but did not improve reading order), and the global reading order is recovered as a degree-constrained directed path cover. To avoid the cascading "edge-theft" failures of greedy edge selection, we propose a max-regret inference rule that prioritizes commitments with high opportunity cost. We evaluate on synthetic Glossa Ordinaria grid layouts, on 23 ALTO page geometries (10 historical source pages plus mirrored and flipped variants), and on a 140-page multi-column English subset of OmniDocBench, comparing our method against the canonical recursive XY-cut (PaddleOCR PP-StructureV3) and two LayoutReader variants (layout-only and text+layout) on identical inputs. On wrap-around Glossa layouts our method recovers 95% of ground-truth successor edges on average vs. XY-cut's 50%; on the OmniDocBench multi-column subset it reaches 88% macro edge accuracy versus XY-cut's 75% and LayoutReader's 25%. The LayoutReader baselines transfer poorly due to a word-level vs. line-level granularity mismatch. We additionally verify mirror-invariance under horizontal and vertical page reflections: Our method changes by less than 1 percentage point, classical XY-cut by 2 points, and LayoutReader-T by up to 8 points.

</details>

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个自动构建公司为中心、环境感知的知识图谱（FinKG-News）方法，并将其用于提升信用风险报告生成的质量和真实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前金融市场受新闻事件影响显著，但事件如何具体影响市场往往未被文本显式表达，因此需要更直观地揭示事件与市场的关系。

Abstract: Financial markets evolve in response to real-world events reported in news, yet these drivers often remain implicit in text. To better explain market dynamics, event-market relations must be explicitly modeled through factual, company-centric, and environment-aware knowledge graphs. We present FinKG-News, a framework that automatically constructs such graphs by extracting news events as anchors linked to companies. Using FinKG-News as grounded evidence that integrates events, news, and company data, we develop an in-context learning architecture for credit risk report generation across three core financial dimensions. Automatic and human evaluations show that automated hallucination detection and quality assessment remain unreliable, making expert judgment indispensable.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 已有研究发现，个性表达适中优于极低或极高，有助于提升信任、乐趣和采纳意向；情境适应性比喻角色优于静态角色，能提升用户体验和使用率。作者基于这些发现提出上述框架。

Conclusion: 通过采用流动性人格框架，可以更好地对齐对话代理的表现与用户需求和多变场景，从而提升其在不同应用中的效果和用户满意度。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based conversational agents (CAs) are now ubiquitous, creating new opportunities for AI-mediated behavior change. Their capacity to project nuanced personalities and adopt diverse metaphorical roles raises a design question: how should an agent's persona and personality be calibrated to the moment? Recent evidence suggests that (i) moderate personality expression outperforms low or high extremes on trust, enjoyment, and intention to adopt in goal-oriented tasks, and (ii) context-appropriate metaphors outperform static one-note assistants on user experience and uptake. Yet most CAs still fix both persona and style, risking misalignment when dynamics, urgency, and formality vary, for example in medical information seeking, fitness coaching, and reflective learning. We propose a Fluid Personality Framework that jointly adapts (1) the agent's metaphorical persona, such as coach, tutor, librarian, or tool, and (2) its personality expression intensity, low, medium, or high, as a function of task context, user goals and traits, and situational urgency. *Elias Najarro,Ane Espeseth,Eleni Nisioti,Sebastian Risi,Stefano Nichele*

TL;DR: 本文认为，大型语言模型（LLM）的集体可以作为人工生命（ALife）的计算基底，通过其相互作用展现复杂的涌现行为，且具备较好的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过赋予多个LLM个体持续记忆、工具、共享技能和自主行动能力，并让它们以自然语言互动，构成具备‘代理性’的智能体集体，系统性梳理和分析这些集体的表现与可解释性。

Result: 作者发现，LLM集体会出现孤立模型中不存在的动态涌现现象；且由于交流基于自然语言，集体行为可被直接追踪或提问，从而提高了系统的可解释性。文中回顾了相关实验与真实部署案例。

Abstract: Complexity and interpretability rarely coincide: systems rich enough for complex behaviours to emerge are usually too opaque to question, while transparent ones are too simple for anything complex to emerge. A single large language model (LLM) is a static artefact, hardly exhibiting any of the emergent properties we associate with life. This changes through interaction: populations of LLMs display emergent dynamics absent from isolated models. Furthermore, LLMs can be endowed with persistent memory, tools and shared skills, and the capacity to initiate actions unprompted, i.e., turning LLMs agentic. In this paper, we argue that such collectives of agents can serve as a computational substrate for Artificial Life (ALife) research. Critically, since the agents communicate in natural language, their collective behaviour can be directly interrogated by examining textual traces and asking the agents themselves. We outline the notion of interpretability in language-model research and extend it for collectives of agents. Lastly, we survey recent examples of agentic LLM collectives that already instantiate the idea of agentic substrates, from controlled experiments to deployments in the wild.

### [194] [Message Passing Enables Efficient Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01077)
*Xuecheng Liu,Daman Arora,Gokul Swamy,Andrea Zanette*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的大型语言模型并行推理框架——消息传递语言模型（MPLMs），通过显式线程间通信（发送/接收消息），减少计算和交换开销，并引入抢占机制提升效率，实现比现有串行和并行方法更高效的长链式推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的链式思维（CoT）等推理增强主要依赖顺序扩展，长链推理计算量大、效率低。最新的Fork-Join（FJ）并行方法虽能分任务多线程处理，但线程间信息沟通有限，影响可扩展性。作者希望突破通信与效率瓶颈，提升LLM并行推理能力。

Method: 提出MPLM（消息传递语言模型）框架，实现在多LLM线程间通过轻量级消息发送/接收（send/receive）实现并行推理，降低上下文冗余和通信成本，并支持根据局部信息早期终止无前景分支（抢占机制）。在多类任务（数独、3-SAT以及问答）上评估MPLM的效率与能力。

Result: 在数独任务中，MPLM的上下文需求比串行CoT和并行FJ更小，并通过单模型微调实现25x25数独解答，结果优于主流方法。在3-SAT任务中，抢占机制有效提高了解题效率。在长上下文问答任务中，大型预训练模型可通过MPLM协议高效推理，表现与FJ接近甚至更优。

Conclusion: MPLM能够高效利用LLM的并行推理能力，降低计算和交互开销，并通过精细化线程间通信和抢占机制提升长链推理效率；实验验证其在多类复杂任务上优于或不逊于现有主流串行和并行方案。

Abstract: While inference-time scaling has improved the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), the need to generate long chains-of-thought (CoTs) is a computational bottleneck. Thus, in contrast to sequential scaling methods like CoT, recent parallel scaling techniques instead use fork and join (FJ) primitives to divide work across multiple LLM threads. However, in the fork-join paradigm, threads are typically transient and do not communicate pointwise with one another which limits scalability. To tackle this, we introduce Message Passing Language Models (MPLMs), a framework for LLM reasoning in which threads communicate directly via lightweight send and receive primitives. MPLMs enable efficient scaling through two key mechanisms: (1) reduced communication costs, achieved by avoiding redundant context sharing, and (2) preemption, which allows threads to terminate early based on partial information from their peers.
  We demonstrate the promise of MPLMs on 3 classes of tasks. First, on Sudoku puzzles, we show that MPLMs require an asymptotically smaller context than both serial CoT and parallel FJ. We then fine-tune a single model to solve 25 x 25 puzzles that remain challenging for standard CoT and FJ approaches, as well as frontier reasoning models without tools. Second, on 3-SAT puzzles, the capability of preemption allows termination of unpromising branches, which results in improved efficiency. Finally, we show that appropriately prompted large pre-trained models follow the MPLM protocol, achieving competitive results on long-context question answering relative to popular fork-join approaches.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: LLM判分虽可达医生水平一致性，但缺乏必要的临床谨慎，不能直接替代医生评卷，评估系统独立性和可靠性必须显式验证，不能仅凭统计一致性。

Abstract: Open-response evaluation provides stronger clinical validity than multiple-choice benchmarks but creates a scoring bottleneck that motivates automated LLM-asa-Judge approaches. Whether such evaluators replicate clinical calibration and caution, however, remains untested. We introduce MedQADE, the first standardised open-response clinical benchmark for German, a major clinical language lacking native evaluation infrastructure, comprising 3,800 items annotated by ten practising physicians and nine Large Language Model (LLM) evaluators. The top-performing evaluator model, Gemini 3 Flash, reached alignment consistent with the physician ceiling (\k{appa} = 0.694 vs. \k{appa} = 0.709), though wide confidence intervals limit interpretation. Despite this statistical alignment, automated evaluators exhibited near-absent clinical metacognition: physicians scaled abstention with item difficulty, while frontier models assigned definitive scores in every case. We additionally quantified systematic lineage-dependent biases, where models preferentially scored architectural siblings, an effect independent of language. These results show that statistical alignment does not ensure clinical caution, and that evaluator independence requires explicit verification.

### [198] [AGC-Bench: Measuring Artificial General Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01152)
*Roger Beaty,Vijeta Deshpande,Clin K. Y. Lai,Anna Attuch,Namrata Shivagunde,Swastik Roy,Rajkumar Pujari,Paul V. DiStefano,Sherin Muckatira,Claire E. Stevenson,Mikhail Gronas,Anna Rumshisky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 这篇论文开发了一个评测大模型创造力的新基准AGC-Bench，并推出创造力评测模型AGC-Judge，为AI创造力提供了公开、系统的测评工具和基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI创造力的问题日益受到关注，但目前缺乏统一且系统的创造力评测基准，存在评测零散、缺乏标准化、对比混乱等痛点。研究动机在于填补这一空白，使创造力的测评更科学、更具可比性，并探讨创造力与领域性和通用智能的关系。

Method: 系统梳理了3101篇AI创造力相关论文，筛选497个评测基准，构建标准化测试集与爬虫工具，推出覆盖78个数据集的AGC-Bench，包含头脑风暴、科学、写作、幽默等多类型任务。针对LLM判分偏差，引入Judge Response Theory纠偏并微调开放模型Qwen3-30B，得到AGC-Judge作为标准打分模型。用该基准测试83个大模型并作因子分析。

Result: 1）主流前沿模型在创造力排行榜领先，开源模型紧随其后。2）因子分析发现存在一个主导的“创造力因子c”，其与通用智能关联但可以区分。3）创造性提示比“推理”提示更有效提升模型创造力得分。4）在人类对比子集下，最佳人类创造力仍优于最佳AI。

Conclusion: 论文构建了首个系统AI创造力评测基准和可开放使用的创造力评判模型，为创造力测量和AI能力分析奠定基础。实验表明AI在部分领域已接近人类水平，但创造力依然有待提升。

Abstract: Creativity research has debated whether creativity is domain-specific (e.g., visual, writing, science), and if it is psychometrically separable from general intelligence. Both questions now apply to LLMs, but a unified benchmark of AI creativity remains elusive. We introduce AGC-Bench, an artificial general creativity benchmark built from a systematic review of the AI creativity literature (3,101 papers screened, 497 benchmarks identified), paired with an agentic harness that converts idiosyncratic codebases into HELM-standardized benchmarks. The first release covers 78 datasets spanning brainstorming, problem solving, STEM, narrative, figurative language, and humor. To address bias in LLM-as-judge, we apply Judge Response Theory -- a psychometric calibration of judge leniency/severity; we then fine-tune Qwen3-30B on the bias-corrected ratings of three frontier LLMs to produce AGC-Judge, an open-weight model that robustly scores new creativity benchmarks it was not trained on. Results reveal frontier models at the top of the AGC-Bench leaderboard, with open models close behind. LLMs show different creative strengths, ranking higher on some domains (e.g., writing) than others (e.g., scientific ideation). Extensive experiments yield three main findings. First, applying factor analysis across 83 LLMs, we recover a single creativity factor 'c', analogous to the 'g' factor of general intelligence, that explains 81.5% of variance, related to but separable from general knowledge/reasoning. Second, we show that prompting models to "be creative" boosts their performance far more than enabling reasoning, evidence that the benchmark tracks creativity over general ability. Third, on a human-matched subset, we find the top human still leads the top LLM on creativity. We release AGC-Bench with a public leaderboard, AGC-Judge, and human data as open infrastructure for measuring AI creativity at scale.

</details>


### [199] [Adversarial Pragmatics for AI Safety Evaluation: A Benchmark for Instruction Conflict, Embedded Commands, and Policy Ambiguity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01153)
*Brett Reynolds*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种名为adversarial pragmatics的新基准和注释协议，用于细致评估大语言模型在复杂语境下的安全性与行为准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的安全评估往往过度简化，将模型行为压缩为“对/错”，不便诊断模型失误背后的真实原因。当前模型在多义语境（如指令冲突、间接语气等）下的表现评判存在不足。

Method: 作者构建了一个包含18个问题的种子基准与54项本地测试案例，结合专家评审流程，对模型在多种语境下的行为进行分类与细粒度标注。同时制定了判别、诊断歧义和分类漂移等评价指标。

Result: 该方法实现了对模型安全性评估维度的精细拆分，能区分任务完成、政策遵从、安全风险、拒绝表现和评审信心等，提升了评估的透明度和专业度。

Conclusion: 论文提出的框架转化了传统语言学判断方法，为大模型安全评测、评委系统建设、金标数据集构建、提示注入测试和安全文档提供了实用工具，显著提升了语言模型行为评估的科学性和实用性。

Abstract: Safety evaluations for language models increasingly depend on judgments about ambiguous natural-language behaviour: whether a model has followed an instruction, refused appropriately, complied with a policy, resisted an embedded command, or misreported progress in an agentic task. Existing benchmarks often compress these distinctions into pass/fail labels, obscuring whether failures arise from capability limits, policy ambiguity, instruction conflict, scaffold failure, or unstable evaluator judgments.
  This paper introduces adversarial pragmatics as a benchmark and annotation protocol for evaluating model behaviour under instruction conflict, embedded commands, quotation, scope ambiguity, deixis, indirect speech acts, and multi-turn agent transcripts. The contribution is empirical and methodological: a linguistically controlled taxonomy, an 18-item seed benchmark with validator-enforced metadata, a 54-row local seed pilot, an expert-evaluation protocol distinguishing task success, policy compliance, safety risk, refusal outcome, and evaluator confidence, and metrics for judge validity, diagnostic ambiguity, and taxonomy drift. The framework turns linguistic judgment methodology into a practical tool for validating safety evals, LLM judges, gold-set construction, prompt-injection tests, and safety documentation.

</details>


### [200] [Distill to Detect: Exposing Stealth Biases in LLMs through Cartridge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01208)
*Shayan Talaei,Abhinav Chinta,Devvrit Khatri,Amin Karbasi,Azalia Mirhoseini,Amin Saberi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新方法Distill to Detect（D2D），能够有效放大和检测语言模型中的隐藏偏见，为实际部署模型的审计提供工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高风险应用场景下，语言模型可能被注入偏见，影响用户决策。尤其危险的是，模型仅在相关话题上展现此偏见，其他输入下表现正常，现有检测方法难以发现这种“隐形”偏见。

Method: 论文提出D2D方法，通过蒸馏嫌疑模型与基准模型输出分布的偏移，将这种偏移浓缩进KV-cache前缀适配器（称为cartridge），从而强化并放大隐藏偏见，使其在生成文本中明显呈现。此外，论文提出理论框架，用Fisher加权映射解释这种放大现象，并给出实验证据支持。

Result: D2D方法能显著放大和揭示多种类型的隐形偏见，极大提升对隐蔽偏见检测的可靠性与实用性。

Conclusion: D2D为审计和检测真实部署语言模型中的隐藏行为提供了行之有效的新途径，对保障模型公正性和安全使用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Language models deployed in high-stakes roles can potentially favor certain entities, brands, or viewpoints, steering user decisions at scale. Such preferential biases can be introduced by any actor in the model's supply chain and are most dangerous when the model reveals its preference only on the relevant topic while behaving identically to its unmodified base on all other inputs. Recent work has shown that these biases can transfer through context distillation on semantically unrelated data, with the signal residing entirely in the soft logit distribution and remaining invisible to text-based inspection. However, the defender faces a fundamental asymmetry: without knowing the bias topic, no detection method can reliably surface a stealth preferential bias, regardless of whether it examines generated text, internal representations, or model weights. Here we introduce Distill to Detect (D2D), a method that surfaces hidden biases by distilling the distributional shift between a suspected model and its base into a cartridge (a KV-cache prefix adapter), concentrating the dominant divergence and amplifying the bias signal into generated text. We show that D2D successfully amplifies the hidden biases of stealth models to the extent that they can be reliably detected across multiple bias types. We also propose a theoretical framework that explains the efficacy of D2D through the lens of Fisher-weighted projection of the logit distribution shift, supported by empirical observations. By turning the capacity bottleneck of prefix-tuning adapters into a detection tool, D2D provides a practical building block for auditing hidden behaviors in deployed language models.

</details>


### [201] [The State-Prediction Separation Hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01218)
*Giovanni Monea,Nathan Godey,Kianté Brantley,Yoav Artzi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出在Transformer架构中分离状态存储与预测两个计算流程的方法，预训练实验表明该方法在数据和算力利用效率上优于标准Transformer，并在下游任务中取得更好表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer在前向传播中兼顾了预测下一个token和存储历史状态的功能，作者认为合并这两种功能可能影响语言建模性能，提出了状态-预测分离假说。

Method: 设计了一种变体Transformer，使用两条独立计算流分别处理状态存储和预测任务，并在不同规模下进行预训练实验。同时通过实证分析排除混杂因素，并对梯度差异进行对比。

Result: 状态-预测分离的Transformer在验证集损失、数据和计算效率方面，持续优于标准Transformer，在下游任务上平均可提升2-3个百分点。

Conclusion: 将状态存储和预测功能分离是提升Transformer性能的有效途径，这种设计带来结构上和梯度上的根本性不同，为未来语言模型架构设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Transformers use the same forward computation stream to both predict the next token and store useful state for future token predictions. We formulate the \emph{state-prediction separation hypothesis}: disentangling the two roles yields better language modeling performance. We design a Transformer variant that uses two computation streams to separate the two functions, and conduct pretraining experiments across various scales. Our experiments show that state-prediction separation consistently offers better data and compute efficiencies, improving validation loss and outperforming standard Transformers by 2--3 percentage points on average on downstream tasks. We also conduct extensive empirical analysis that rules out potential confounders and demonstrates the fundamental difference in the gradients our design entails.

</details>


### [202] [Measuring the Gap Between Human and LLM Research Ideas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01233)
*Ziyu Chen,Yilun Zhao,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种评估大语言模型（LLM）生成研究创意与真实人类学者之间差异的新框架，并揭示LLM生成的创意分布范围较窄、系统性偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前评估LLM创意多聚焦单个点如新颖性或可行性，但缺乏对其与人类学者整体研究取向差距的系统性分析。作者想回答LLM生成的创意与真实人类研究创意之间存在多大差异。

Method: 作者建立了一个基于高质量论文、可大规模自动化的评估体系。首先，逆向推理每篇论文背后的关键先行工作集合，用LLM依据这些先行工作生成新创意。然后，提出双轴研究品味分类法，将创意按机会模式和研究范式刻画，通过量化描述LLM与人类创意的分布差异。

Result: 各类LLM生成的研究创意普遍偏集中于桥接型机会和综合方法，相较于人类论文参考分布，LLM的创意覆盖范围更窄且存在系统性分布偏移。

Conclusion: 尽管LLM能够给出多样且合理的研究想法，但仍难以覆盖人类丰富多元的选题视角，研究取向也有显著偏离。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly used to brainstorm research ideas, but existing evaluations mostly judge individual ideas by novelty, feasibility, or expert preference. We instead ask: how far are current LLM-generated ideas from human researchers? To characterize this gap, we build a large-scale evaluation framework for ideation from high-quality human research papers. For each paper, we reverse-engineer a small set of closely related prior works that likely inspired its core idea. LLMs are then prompted to generate a new idea from the set of paper titles and summaries. We introduce a two-axis research-taste taxonomy to profile each idea by its opportunity pattern and research paradigm, and use it to quantify the divergence between human and LLM ideas. Across idea sets generated by different LLMs, we observe a consistent distributional gap: LLM ideas are disproportionately concentrated around bridge-like opportunities and synthesis methods, whereas the human paper reference distribution spreads more broadly across ways of framing gaps and constructing contributions. This result suggests that strong LLMs can produce a range of reasonable ideas, but that range remains narrower than, and systematically shifted relative to, human research taste.

</details>

### [203] [EmbodimentSemantic: A Spatial Scene-Graph Dataset and Benchmark for Vision-Language Models on Embodied Manipulation Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00020)
*Hassan Jaber,Refinath S N,Luca Cagliero,Christopher E. Mower,Haitham Bou-Ammar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了EmbodimentSemantic空间场景图数据集和基准，以评估机器人操作中视觉-语言-动作系统(VLA)的空间关系理解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA系统尽管能够识别物体和解析语言指令，但缺乏对物体空间排列（如支撑、包含、遮挡、顺序和深度）的明确建模，这限制了其在机器人操作中的应用。

Method: 作者构建了EmbodimentSemantic数据集，将场景表示为有向的物体-关系-物体三元组（scene graph），每个三元组用一组固定的空间关系描述一对物体的空间联系，支持对空间绑定、关系预测和一致性的直接评估。数据涵盖真实机器人操作录像（SO101机械臂）和仿真环境下的大规模框架LIBERO，实现了自动推导空间关系。还通过将scene graph注入现有VLA策略，检验其对机器人操作控制的帮助。

Result: 实验结果表明，当前视觉-语言模型能预测出合理的空间关系，但在处理需要准确深度及视点相关的空间结构时表现不佳。

Conclusion: EmbodimentSemantic为分析和提升VLM模型的空间理解能力、及其在实际机器人操作任务中的应用效果提供了统一框架和重要基准。

Abstract: Spatial grounding remains a key limitation of vision-language-action (VLA) systems for robotic manipulation. While current models can recognize objects and follow language instructions, they often lack an explicit representation of how objects are arranged in space, including support, containment, ordering, occlusion, and depth-sensitive relations. We introduce EmbodimentSemantic, a spatial scene-graph dataset and benchmark for evaluating relational grounding in embodied manipulation. EmbodimentSemantic represents scenes as directed object-relation-object triplets, where each triplet specifies a spatial relation between an ordered pair of objects using a fixed set of relations. This representation enables direct evaluation of object binding, relation prediction, and spatial consistency. The dataset includes real-world manipulation observations collected with the low-cost SO101 robot arm, together with generated scene graphs for studying spatial grounding in practical robotic settings. To provide controlled validation, we also introduce a simulator-grounded LIBERO benchmark with over 60K manipulation frames and more than 120K camera-specific scene graphs across paired third-person and wrist views, where ground-truth relations are derived automatically from MuJoCo geometry, world coordinates, camera projections, and visibility constraints. We further test whether scene graphs improve downstream control by injecting them into existing VLA policy prompts. Experiments across open-source and commercial VLMs show that current models often predict plausible relations but struggle with exact depth-aware and viewpoint-dependent spatial structure. EmbodimentSemantic provides a unified framework for diagnosing spatial grounding in VLM perception and testing its utility for VLA manipulation.

</details>


### [204] [When to Personalize Household Object Search: A Rigidity-Gated Hybrid Policy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00022)
*Xianyao Li,Yuhai Wang,Hu Xiao,Kaleb Smith,Gilbert Yang Ye,Eric Jing Du*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在家用服务机器人中根据住户特质实现物体搜索个性化的混合策略PerSim，并利用人类校准的仿真数据进行训练与验证。结果表明：对于摆放行为可变的物品，个性化显著提升搜索效果；对于摆放位置固定的物品，常规频次策略表现良好。PerSim整体降低了搜索成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 服务机器人在家庭环境中搜索物品时，依赖于空间先验知识来降低搜索成本，但不同住户的物品位置随个体特质变化，采集大量特质相关的真实轨迹既侵犯隐私又难以规模化，因此需要新的解决方法。

Method: 提出了PerSim，一个由特质条件化先验和群体频率基线组成的混合策略，仅在摆放行为多变时进行个性化。为扩大数据，利用人类校准的仿真模拟生成对象摆放转移轨迹，并训练预测器以连续Big Five人格特质向量输出房间级先验与房内共现线索。通过人类理解测试和A/B盲测，以及数字孪生家庭环境中的离线性能评估验证策略有效性。

Result: 人类评估认为仿真生成对象移动轨迹行为可信（均值3.85/5，极显著），A/B测试中，个性化对低固定度物品更受青睐（p=0.005），高固定度物品群体频率法稳健。连续特质向量预测优于离散特质配置（p=0.035）。PerSim在数字孪生家庭实际场景中减少了整体搜索成本。

Conclusion: PerSim框架能有效动态决策何时为住户进行个性化物品搜索，降低搜索成本。在五维人格特质空间的插值能力为服务机器人个性化提供新途径，对于提升家庭服务机器人的用户体验和效率具有实际意义。

Abstract: Service robots searching for household objects rely on spatial priors to reduce search cost, yet object locations can vary with resident traits. Collecting longitudinal, trait-specific in-home trajectories is invasive and hard to scale. We study when personalization helps and propose PerSim, a rigidity-gated hybrid policy that combines a trait-conditioned prior with a population-frequency baseline, personalizing only when placement behavior is variable. To scale resident-conditioned dynamics, we employ a human-calibrated simulation pipeline to generate and validate object-placement transitions in diverse home layouts, and train a predictor that injects continuous Big Five vectors to output room-level priors and within-room co-occurrence cues. In a unified human study (N=200), dual-layer validation shows that (i) synthetic transitions are judged behaviorally plausible (mean 3.85/5, p < 1e-6), and (ii) in a blinded A/B comparison, personalization is favored primarily for low-rigidity objects (p=0.005), while the population-frequency baseline remains strong for universally placed items, yielding a decision rule for when to personalize. In an offline objective test, we observe a small but significant improvement on unseen continuous trait vectors over nearest discrete configuration matching (p=0.035), supporting interpolation in five-dimensional trait space. Finally, in a home digital twin we show that PerSim reduces expected search cost by combining room visitation effort with within-room cue checking, demonstrating end-to-end gains beyond isolated prediction metrics.

</details>


### [205] [Decentralized Geometric Control for Cable-Suspended Payload Transport with Adaptive Mass Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00024)
*Hadi Hajieghrary,Benedikt Walter,Paul Schmitt,Miguel Hurtado*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出一种无需中央协调且安全高效的多无人机协作空中运输新方法。通过让每个无人机基于自身传感自行估算负载分担，实现了隐式协作，保障了运行安全，且控制精度高、计算开销小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多架无人机协同运输悬索负载时，面临要兼顾非线性动力学、安全约束、并且不能依赖中心化协调和高频通信的问题。现有方法普遍需要集中式控制或较多通信，难以应用于实际有约束、噪声和不确定性的环境。

Method: 本文提出了GPAC——一种四层层次结构的控制框架。每个四旋翼仅通过本地缆绳状态自主估算自身所分担的负载，无需获知总无人机数或负载质量。集成了几何位置与姿态控制、抗摆动机制、抗风扩展状态观测器、基于并发学习的质量估计（无需持续激励），以及按优先级排序的控制屏障函数安全滤波；仅需低频邻居位置广播进行防撞。

Result: 提出的GPAC框架能够在高保真模拟环境下（含柔性缆绳、板载传感器融合和风扰动），在所有控制和估计回路闭环的条件下实现平均33.8厘米的负载跟踪均方根误差（13组种子系数变异仅2.8%），每架无人机计算成本很低。

Conclusion: GPAC实现了分布式的多无人机协作运输，无需中心化协调、信息交换极少，确保安全的同时能精确控制负载轨迹；控制方法理论上能保障非线性稳定性，且具高实用性与扩展性。

Abstract: Cooperative aerial transport requires controllers that respect nonlinear manifold geometry, operate without centralized coordination, and respect operational safety constraints. To address these demands, we present GPAC, a four-layer hierarchical architecture that enables $N$ quadrotors to transport a cable-suspended payload without a central coordinator or by exchanging cable states or adaptive parameters. The key insight is implicit coordination: each quadrotor independently estimates its effective load share from local cable measurements, so combined forces converge to the correct total, even without knowledge of $N$ or the payload mass; the payload position is reconstructed locally from each agent's own cable geometry, and the only inter-agent communication is a low-rate neighbor-position broadcast for collision avoidance. GPAC operates directly on the full nonlinear configuration manifold and integrates geometric position and attitude control, anti-swing regulation, an extended-state observer for wind rejection, concurrent learning-based mass estimation without persistent excitation, and a priority-ordered control barrier function (CBF)-inspired safety filter that reduces operational risk, with input-to-state safety (ISSf) margins that hold exactly under single-constraint activation. A compatibility result shows that the filter's force modifications keep the desired attitude within the almost-global stability region of the $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ attitude controller. Finally, high-fidelity simulation with flexible cables, onboard sensor fusion, and wind turbulence -- with all control and estimation loops closed through the estimator -- yields a mean payload-tracking RMSE of 33.8 cm (2.8\% coefficient of variation over 13 seeds) at a low per-agent computational cost.

</details>


### [206] [FLYNN: Robust Neural Network for Robot Navigation using Fly Brain Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00025)
*Benquan Wang,Jingdao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文基于果蝇（Drosophila melanogaster）大脑连接组，提出了一种新型RNN结构（FLYNN），表现出比现有网络更强的鲁棒性和适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习模型在新环境或感官缺失时易脆弱，而生物大脑具有强大容错性。作者旨在探索生物大脑连接结构对网络鲁棒性的贡献。

Method: 直接以果蝇大脑连接组为基础设计RNN结构，并训练其在MuJoCo平台进行基于视觉的导航任务，同时与传统手工设计神经网络进行性能比较。

Result: FLYNN在导航任务中的表现与参数量相近的现代网络相当，但在分布外数据和感官丧失（如失明）情况下表现更好。主成分分析显示其内部表征具有高度模块化。

Conclusion: 基于生物连接组的神经网络结构可大幅提升网络鲁棒性，为构建更具适应性的人工智能系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: While deep learning models achieve state-of-the-art performance in complex tasks, they remain brittle when faced with new environments or sensory deprivation. In contrast, biological systems exhibit remarkable tolerance to these challenges. We address this vulnerability by developing a recurrent neural network (RNN) whose architecture is directly derived from the synaptic-resolution brain connectome of the fruit fly Drosophila melanogaster. We demonstrate the feasibility of training the fly connectome neural network (FLYNN) to perform vision-based navigation in MuJoCo, achieving performance comparable to modern hand-crafted networks of similar parameter counts. Crucially, FLYNN exhibits superior resistance to out-of-distribution (OOD) data and tolerance to sensory loss without further training. It remained functional even under total vision loss while hand-crafted networks largely failed, even when specifically trained with camera dropout. Principal Component Analysis (PCA) of the internal state of FLYNN suggests that it exhibits a particularly high degree of representational modularity, which might be related to its robustness. Our work provides a new direction for designing resilient artificial agents following the topology of biological brains.

### [207] [Invariant Stochastic Filtering on SE(3) for Inertial-Encoder State Estimation of Serial Rigid Manipulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00026)
*S. Yaqubi,J. Mattila*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在Lie群SE(3)上专门为多连杆刚性机械臂设计的不变量扩展卡尔曼滤波器（IEKF），并验证了其稳定性和数值有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于任意连杆数的串联刚性机械臂，传统的状态估计算法面临精度、稳定性和可扩展性挑战，尤其是在系统非线性及高自由度情形。作者希望在保证模块化和可扩展性的前提下，提高估计精度与鲁棒性。

Method: 作者将整个状态估计问题表述在SE(3)的Lie群结构下，利用运动学方程的群仿射特性，使线性化误差动力学成为自治系统。采用物理分离的噪声模型独立处理陀螺仪和加速度计通道。滤波器按连杆模块化链式组织，前置连杆的后验通过伴随变换影响预测协方差，实现线性计算复杂度。采用Lie代数Lyapunov函数建立了均方意义下的指数有界性，并通过伴随算子范数链式传递，实现可扩展的稳定性证明。

Result: 构建的IEKF在数值仿真中效果良好，能够准确估计多连杆机械臂状态，且理论上证明了其可以扩展到任意数量的连杆。

Conclusion: 提出的方法不仅在理论上实现了鲁棒性和可扩展性，而且实际仿真显示其具有良好精度。IEKF的模块化结构使其适用于大规模多连杆机械臂系统。

Abstract: An invariant extended Kalman filter (IEKF) is developed for state estimation of serial rigid manipulators with an arbitrary number of links, formulated entirely within the Lie group SE(3). The group-affine property of the kinematic equations makes the linearised error dynamics autonomous, so the Riccati equation governs the true error covariance rather than a local approximation. A physically separated noise model treats gyroscope and accelerometer channels independently: the accelerometer provides translational twist via gravity-compensated integration, yielding a measurement covariance that scales with the sample interval in exact analogy with process noise discretisation; a state-dependent Coriolis noise term captures gyroscope noise propagating through the nonlinear dynamics, vanishing at rest and growing with twist magnitude. The filter is structured as a modular chain of per-link IEKFs in which the predicted covariance of each link depends on its predecessor only through the Adjoint-transformed posterior, giving linear computational cost in link count. Exponential ultimate boundedness in mean square is established via a Lie algebra Lyapunov function, with per-link bounds chained through the Adjoint operator norm to yield a stability certificate that is modular and scalable to arbitrary chain length. Numerical results validate the design.

</details>


### [208] [Urban Deceleration Behavior Modes Under Scene Context: An Early-Kinematic Classifier from Argoverse 2 Multi-Agent Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00027)
*Eni Solomon Laughter*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本研究对城市跟车行为中的减速模式进行了分类和预测，发现城市减速主要呈现出四类稳定行为模式。文中使用真实自动驾驶数据、聚类分析和机器学习方法，从运动学特征和场景变量角度分析影响减速的主要因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然城市环境下车辆减速的行为被大量实证研究，但对其行为类别的系统归纳仍较为缺乏。借助自动驾驶感知数据，可以更细致地分析和组织减速行为的模式。

Method: 利用Argoverse 2 Sensor数据集，从234份城市驾驶记录中提取了1219个持续减速事件，并以19维运动学特征对每个事件编码。用K-means聚类分析结合自助法稳定性检验寻找行为模式，并通过梯度提升分类器预测事件发生初期的行为模式。还分析了11个场景上下文变量对模式的调节作用。

Result: 共识别出四种主要且稳定的减速行为模式：预判型减速(62.8%)、被动接近型(30.6%)、刹车型跃变(4.8%)和极少数异常型(1.8%)。场景变量中仅配对车辆“年龄”表现出中等影响，其他比如场景几何和弱势用路者距离影响甚微。基于事件前1秒特征预测模式的宏F1可达0.758。

Abstract: Urban deceleration is one of the most empirically studied yet least taxonomically organized behaviors in car-following research. Recent perception-equipped autonomous-vehicle datasets enable trajectory-anchored mode discovery. We extract 1,219 sustained deceleration events from 234 urban driving logs of the Argoverse 2 Sensor dataset, encode each event in a 19-dimensional kinematic feature vector, discover behavioral modes via K-means clustering with bootstrap stability analysis, and quantify modulation by eleven scene-context variables. A HistGradientBoosting classifier predicts mode membership from the first 1.0 s of each event. Four stable modes emerge with a bootstrap Adjusted Rand Index of 0.897 across 50 resamples: anticipatory soft (62.8%), reactive closing (30.6%), brake-like jerk (4.8%), and an outlier category (1.8%). Only pair age shows a medium effect (epsilon^2 = 0.085); scene geometry and vulnerable-road-user proximity show negligible effects. The early-event classifier achieves macro-F1 = 0.758 at 1.0 s, with scene context contributing +0.059 F1 over kinematics alone. Modes are regime-invariant in medium-speed driving (ARI = 0.817) but regime-dependent at low speed (ARI = 0.166). A small set of stable kinematic modes structures urban deceleration; early-window jerk dominates predictive signal; and pair age is the primary contextual modulator.

Imitation Learning offers direct training from real-world data but lacks modeling of social interactions and suffers from error accumulation. To this end, we propose an imitation learning framework that leverages spatiotemporal dynamics for socially compliant navigation. To represent social context based on interactions, we introduce a graph-based auxiliary network that encodes crowd states by attending to pedestrians. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么只根据外观区分类别，导致无法区分外观相似但行为不同的物体，要么基于预设动作的效果分类，泛化性和灵活性不足。因此，亟需一种既能自动学习操作原语又能发现物体类别、基于实际交互结果的泛化方法。

Method: 提出一种包含二值瓶颈层的模型，能够通过预测物体运动、接触和力反馈等多模态效果，从随机交互数据中联合学习高层操作原语和物体类别，并基于效果轨迹的中间步骤结合离散规划，实现更精细的低层控制。同时，通过少量效果比对实现对新物体的类行为泛化。

Abstract: To perform complex manipulation planning, autonomous robots are required to abstract continuous, high-dimensional sensorimotor interactions into discrete object and action representations. Earlier work either categorized objects based on visual appearances, which fails to distinguish objects that appear similar but behave differently, or based on effects under interaction, but was limited to predefined actions. To address these limitations, we propose a model that jointly discovers high-level manipulation primitives and object categories through a binary bottleneck layer, trained to predict multi-modal outcomes, including object motion, contact, and force feedback, from random interaction data. Building on these discovered binary representations, we leverage a discrete planning method that uses intermediate steps in the predicted effect trajectory to enable partial action executions for precise low-level control. Additionally, we evaluate our framework's generalization capabilities on novel objects by assigning object categories through comparing a small number of interaction effects with the predicted effects of learned object symbols, enabling few-shot generalization based on behavior rather than visual similarity. We conduct experiments on tabletop repositioning and stacking tasks, and confirm that our effect-driven planning approach outperforms both a state-of-the-art method and a visual-based alternative in planning precision across seen and novel objects.

### [213] [Learning Dexterous Manipulation Using Contact Wrench Guidance From Human Demonstration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00033)
*Xinghao Zhu,Zixi Liu,Shalin Jain,Chenran Li,Milad Noori,Huihua Zhao,John Welsh,Michael Andres Lin,Wei Liu,Tingwu Wang,Xingye Da,Zhengyi Luo,Vishal Kulkarni,Naema Bhatti,Yuke Zhu,Linxi Fan,Bowen Wen,Danfei Xu,Soha Pouya,Yan Chang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出CHORD框架，通过关注物体受力（力和力矩）实现了将人类操作演示迁移到机器人灵巧操控任务，并用大量任务验证了其高效性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人灵巧操作如果能充分利用丰富的真人操作演示，将极大提升学习效率和实际能力，但人机差异导致示范迁移一直存在困难。

Method: 作者提出CHORD框架，核心思想是以物体为中心，将人或机器人动作统一表达为对物体施加的力和力矩（contact wrench），并通过这种物理量指导强化学习，有效度量演示和机器人的相似性。此外，作者建立了4,739个双手操控任务的大规模模拟基准，采用动作捕捉和自制视频生成数据。

Result: 在1,831个基准任务上，CHORD平均成功率达82.12%；还能将手部或第三方演示泛化到全身操作，成功率达90.77%。此外，所学策略能迁移到真实世界的开环和闭环设置。

Conclusion: 通过以物理量为媒介的演示指导，CHORD大幅提升了复杂触觉操作的可扩展性和迁移性，为机器人模仿学习与强化学习结合开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Dexterous robot manipulation can benefit from the abundance of human demonstrations, but transferring such demonstrations to robot policies remains challenging. We present Contact Wrench Guidance from Human Demonstration in Robotic Dexterous Manipulation (CHORD), a framework for long-horizon manipulation of rigid and articulated objects with reinforcement learning. The key idea is object-centric contact wrench space guidance: we represent human and robot motions by the forces and torques they can induce on the object, enabling similarity to be measured by the induced instantaneous motions. This guidance makes reinforcement learning more scalable for contact-rich dexterous manipulation. We further introduce a large-scale simulation benchmark with 4,739 bimanual dexterous manipulation tasks, constructed from motion-capture datasets and reconstructed in-house videos. Evaluated on 1,831 benchmark tasks, CHORD achieves an average success rate of 82.12%, demonstrating strong scalability. CHORD also generalizes to whole-body manipulation from hand-only and third-person demonstrations, achieving a 90.77% success rate, and the learned policies transfer to the real world in both open-loop and closed-loop settings.

### [214] [Optimal any-angle path planning in static and dynamic environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00065)
*Yiyuan Zou,Clark Borst*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大部分任意角度路径规划算法无法在动态障碍物存在时保证最优性，且计算开销较大。本文旨在开发既能保证最优解又能高效运行的通用路径规划方法，适用于各种实际场景（如空域、仓库、海洋等）。

Method: 本文提出两种加速并保持最优性的通用技术：1）椭圆前向扩展，利用椭圆型邻域限制搜索空间；2）视野法，替代传统视线检查方式提升可见性判断效率。引入了正向扫描与反向扫描两种可整合上述技术的扫描策略。基于此，开发了Zeta*（静态环境）和Zeta*-SIPP（动态环境）算法。

Result: Zeta*算法在静态环境下性能与Anya算法持平，并易于拓展到动态环境。Zeta*-SIPP在静态和动态环境下均展现出高效率，其速度比当前最优的TO-AA-SIPP算法快20倍以上。

Conclusion: 本文总结了最优任意角度路径规划的核心需求，并提出了一种适用于多种环境的统一高效方案，为动态和静态场景下的路径规划提供了更优选择。

Abstract: Any-angle path planning extends traditional graph-based path planning by allowing movement between any pair of vertices, rather than being restricted by predefined edges. It can find straighter and shorter paths in continuous space with graphs, making it particularly suitable for navigation in open areas such as airspaces, warehouses, and oceans. Many any-angle path-planning algorithms have been proposed, but only a few can guarantee optimal solutions, especially in the presence of dynamic obstacles. To address this challenge, this article focuses on optimal any-angle path planning on grids and introduces two general techniques that accelerate computation while preserving optimality in both static and dynamic environments: 1) elliptical forward expansion, which leverages ellipse-based neighborhoods to restrict the search space, and 2) field of view, which replaces traditional line-of-sight methods to speed up visibility checks. To integrate these two techniques, inverted and forward scanning are introduced. Inverted scanning establishes visual connections from open nodes, whereas forward scanning initiates scans from closed nodes. Building on the proposed techniques, Zeta* and Zeta*-SIPP are developed for static and dynamic environments respectively. Zeta*, when combined with forward scanning, is similar to the state-of-the-art algorithm Anya and attains comparable performance. Unlike Anya, Zeta* can be readily extended to other settings, such as dynamic environments (e.g., Zeta*-SIPP). Zeta*-SIPP, with either scanning method, is more than 20 times faster than the corresponding state-of-the-art optimal planner TO-AA-SIPP. Overall, this research identifies the key requirements for achieving optimal any-angle path planning and introduces a unified approach suitable for different environments.

This module ensures that robot movements strictly adhere to expert operational norms, real-time kinematic limits, and vessel safety constraints. Furthermore, a 13% reduction in trajectory variance indicates superior procedural standardization, aligning autonomous behavior with established clinical norms. ### [216] [AD-MPCC: Adaptive Differentiable Model Predictive Contouring Control for Autonomous Racing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00141)
*Nam T. Nguyen,Binh Nguyen,Ahmad Amine,Thanh Vo-Duy,Rahul Mangharam,Truong X. Nghiem*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了自适应可微分模型预测切线控制（AD-MPCC）框架，通过结合可微MPCC与在线参数估计，实现对不同道路表面条件的适应，提升无人赛车的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人赛车控制方法难以有效应对路面状况变化，且很难实时自适应调节控制器权重，导致性能和安全性受限。

Method: 1. 基于Pacejka 魔术公式的参数化轮胎模型，采用带有正则化和指数衰减权重的滑动窗口在线估计方案，动态捕捉路面交互变化。
2. 提出可微分MPCC（Diff-MPCC），允许根据长时域性能目标动态地自适应调优控制器权重。
3. 用Pacejka模型辅助的机器学习方法进行权重学习，结合Diff-MPCC生成的数据进行有监督训练。

Result: 仿真结果显示，所提AD-MPCC框架无论在单一或多变的路况下，均能显著提升安全性，并使无人赛车圈速优于基线控制器。

Conclusion: AD-MPCC通过结合在线参数估计和自适应权重调整，实现了高效安全的无人赛车控制，对复杂多变道路环境表现出优越的鲁棒性与速度优势。

Abstract: This paper presents Adaptive Differentiable Model Predictive Contouring Control (AD-MPCC), a framework for autonomous racing that integrates differentiable MPCC with online parameter estimation to handle varying road-surface conditions. For online parameter estimation, we leverage a parameterized Pacejka Magic Formula together with a regularized moving-horizon estimation scheme with exponentially decaying weights to capture road interactions and update parameters in real time. Furthermore, we propose a differentiable MPCC (Diff-MPCC) framework that enables optimal adjustment of objective weights based on predefined long-horizon performance costs. To implement Diff-MPCC for online objective weight adaptation, we propose a Pacejka-informed machine learning model that is trained in a supervised manner using data generated by Diff-MPCC to tune the objective weights. Simulation results demonstrate that AD-MPCC reliably ensures safety and achieves faster lap times compared to baseline controllers in both single-surface and multiple-surface scenarios.

</details>

<details>
